This file contains the multiplicities of rhobars (p=5) occuring newly at level N^2 with N=-1 (mod 5) and N<200.
The format of the data is [m,f] where m is the multiplicity and the eigenvalues are in F_{p^f} and then the system
of eigenvalues (mod p)
